***сковать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́ть</a> (12475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковать.html>кова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сковывать.html>ско́вывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to forge, to hammer out</li>
<li>to forge together</li>
<li>to chain</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hold, to fix
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>огнём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skovátʹ</b> ognjóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pin (down) by fire</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratevly<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with ice</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lock, to beset
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мороз.html>моро́з</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:лед.html>лёд</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>ре́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">moróz/ljod <b>skovál</b> réku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the river is frozen over; the river is icebound</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fetter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>страх</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">strax <b>skovál</b> mne dúšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I was overcome/seized with fear</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>ско́ванный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skóvannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скованность.html>ско́ванность</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skóvannostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковать.html>кова́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***сковывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сковывать.html>ско́вывать</a> (17803)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сковывать.html>ско́вывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skóvyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to forge, to hammer out</li>
<li>to forge together</li>
<li>to chain</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hold, to fix
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сковывать.html>ско́вывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>огнём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skóvyvatʹ</b> ognjóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pin (down) by fire</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(with ice)</i> to lock</li>
<li>to fetter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>страх</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>скова́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">strax <b>skovál</b> mne dúšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I was overcome/seized with fear</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сковать.html>ско́ванный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skóvannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скованность.html>ско́ванность</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skóvannostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковать.html>кова́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кованый.html>ко́ваный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kóvanyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ко́вкий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kóvkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ко́вка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kóvka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***скок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скок.html>скок</a> (25513)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*skokъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скок.html>скок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скок.html>ско́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скок.html>ско́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скок.html>ско́ков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gallop</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скок.html>скок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skok</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">familiar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> jump, skip, hop
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:скок.html>скок</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ль</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oná <b>skok</b> k nemú v postélʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">she hopped right into his bed</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***сколачивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сколачивать.html>скола́чивать</a> (27751)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколотить.html>сколоти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skolotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколачивать.html>скола́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skoláčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколотить.html>сколоти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to knock together
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколачивать.html>скола́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ящик.html>я́щик</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>досок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skoláčivatʹ</b> jáščik iz dosok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to knock up a box</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to knock together, to knit together
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколачивать.html>скола́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:группа.html>гру́ппу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skoláčivatʹ</b> grúppu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to knock together a group</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***сколотить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сколотить.html>сколоти́ть</a> (10735)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колотить.html>колоти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколотить.html>сколоти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skolotítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколачивать.html>скола́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to knock together
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколотить.html>сколоти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ящик.html>я́щик</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>до́сок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skolotítʹ</b> jáščik iz dósok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to knock up a box</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to knock together, to knit together
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколотить.html>сколоти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:группа.html>гру́ппу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skolotítʹ</b> grúppu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to knock together a group</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколотить.html>сколоти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:состояние.html>состоя́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skolotítʹ</b> sostojánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to scrape together [scrape up; knock up] a fortune</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***скользить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скользить.html>скользи́ть</a> (4615)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ско́льз(<a href = vnd.unilang:кий.html>кий</a>)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skólʹz(kij)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользить.html>скользи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skolʹzítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользнуть.html>скользну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to slide, to slip</li>
<li>to glide</li>
<li>to float</li></ol>

***скользкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скользкий.html>ско́льзкий</a> (5576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*ко́льзкий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*kólʹzkij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slippery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ко́льзко</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kólʹzko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is attested), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">кользъкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolĭzŭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">сковзки́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skovzkýj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slippery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">ко́взати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kóvzaty</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to slip</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Additionally cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kiełzać</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stumble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Per Vasmer, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kъlz-</i>, of unknown further origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользкий.html>ско́льзкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skólʹzkij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ско́льзче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>slippery, dangerous <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a surface</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>slimy</li></ol>

<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:склизкий.html>скли́зкий</a></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:ненадежный.html>ненадёжный</a>, двусмысленный, <a href = vnd.unilang:сомнительный.html>сомни́тельный</a></li>

***скользнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скользнуть.html>скользну́ть</a> (5021)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">скълъзнути</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skŭlŭznuti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically derived from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользить.html>скользи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skolʹzítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользнуть.html>скользну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skolʹznútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользить.html>скользи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to slide, to slip</li>
<li>to glide</li>
<li>to float</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sneak <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">into, by</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to graze <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative, someone/something; of a bullet</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***сколько.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> (244)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">колико</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">koliko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*koliko</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skólʹko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>how much, how many
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>сто́ит</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Skólʹko</b> éto stóit?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How much does this cost?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Skólʹko</b> u vas knig?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How many books do you have?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Skólʹko</b> vam let?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How old are you?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́льких</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:умереть.html>у́мер</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Skólʹkix</b> let on úmer?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">At what age did he die?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>so much, so many
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зима.html>зи́м</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Skólʹko</b> let, <b>skólʹko</b> zim!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It’s been ages since we met!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́льких</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учителе́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́лся</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U <b>skólʹkix</b> učiteléj ja učílsja!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’ve studied with so many teachers!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>how long
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ждать.html>ждать</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Skólʹko</b> mne ješčó ždatʹ?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How long do I still have to wait?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Before uncountable nouns, only nominative and accusative are used.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сконструировать.html>сконструи́ровать</a> (17130)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конструировать.html>конструи́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">konstruírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сконструировать.html>сконструи́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skonstruírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конструировать.html>конструи́ровать</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сконцентрировать.html>сконцентри́ровать</a> (18799)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:концентрировать.html>концентри́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">koncentrírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сконцентрировать.html>сконцентри́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skoncentrírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:концентрировать.html>концентри́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to concentrate, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mass</li></ol>

***скоп.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скоп.html>скоп</a> (19401)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скоп.html>скоп</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skop</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скоп.html>ско́па</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скоп.html>ско́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скоп.html>ско́пов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> group, accumulation; stock, savings</li></ol>
